    Introduction

    This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

    As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

    Base URL

    http://smallchops.test

    Authenticating requests

    This API is not authenticated.

    Endpoints

    Authenticate users

    Example request:

    curl -X POST \
    "http://smallchops.test/api/login" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -H "Accept: application/json"
    const url = new URL(
    "http://smallchops.test/api/login"
);

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
    Received response:
    Request failed with error:

    Request      

    POST api/login

    Authenticate admin users

    Example request:

    -H "Accept: application/json"

    Confirms Token

    Example request:

    curl -X GET \
    -G "http://smallchops.test/api/reset-password/qui" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -H "Accept: application/json"
    const url = new URL(
    "http://smallchops.test/api/reset-password/qui"
);

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

    Request      

    GET api/reset-password/{token}

    URL Parameters

    token  string  

    Resets Password

    Example request:

    curl -X POST \
    "http://smallchops.test/api/reset-password" \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -H "Accept: application/json"
    const url = new URL(
    "http://smallchops.test/api/reset-password"
);

let headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());

    POST api/send-reset-token

    Generate a new token for user

    Example request:

    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
